via, teten qualac via: motetia

Tla tlauh quj azcatl, anoço

Quauh azcatl: itech mj toa

ma chaloa, hiiaia, velia.(920)

Coztic yie suchitl: çan  no ie
hoatl: iece coztic, velic, aviac, 

tlacotli, tetonal, teiol qujma in
in çan  iuh qujn xivitl, çan  iuh qujn
tlacotl. Auh in ce quj nexpa in 
ca quja, yoan nextli injc quj tzin 
tlal pachoa; in tzoiac yie suchitl 
ic cocavia, ic mocuepa; cocauh 
quj suchitl, ic velia, a viaia.(921)

Quauh yie suchitl: tla tlacotic 
memelactic, memelaoac, popo 
conj nj, mamalacachi vinj, qujl
lo, veveiac, qujllo papa tlaoac, 
totomaoac inj tlacoio, iticoion 
quj, itipochin quj. Inj suchio vi
viac, xo xouh quj, xoxoctic, vi
via quja, maci, icuci.(922)

Chal chiuh suchitl: çan  no 
iehoatl, in quauh yie suchitl: 
ipampa in xoxoctic, in chalchi
uhtic, in xoxocpatic, xim mal
tic: hiiaia, velia, coceoa, ca mj
livi.(923)

Chalchiuh yie suchitl: çan  no 
iehoatl in omjto, chalchiuhtic, 
texocaltic, maviztic, mavicauh
quj, elevilizio, nene qujztli, ne
qujztli, neneconj, neconj, nene
conj.(924)

Tzoiac yie suchitl; çan  ie ie
hoatl inj ie suchitl, ie ce tzoiac 
oxiio, tzoiaia.(925)

    fo. 194

Azcal suchitl, iuh qujn tolin

Iopi suchitl, iztac, tla tlapal hoa
oan quj, macouh quj, mj mj ia oa
io, tomjollo, mala cachtic: inj
quauh io iuh qujn itz tolin, ma
la cach tontli, atlan in mochioa, 
omjto.(926)

Vacal suchitl: inj quauhio 
me mecatic, motla tlamj nanj, 
ama tlapale: qujllo papa tlaoac 
inj atlapal iuh qujn, aio cona,
tetz caltic, ia man quj, tla tlalhoa
io, vi viac inj quauhio: inj atla
pal mo vilananj, mo vico manj, 
mo ia ca tlacanj; inj suchio mj
mjltic, ititza ian quj: inj itic hi
cac, ino cceppa yiollo, ololtic, 
ia ca vitztic: oxio. In in suchitl 
inj eo aio tilaoac, mo vilana, me
catic, meme catic, memecati, 
mj cuja.(927)

Tecciz oacal suchitl: toma
oac inj quauhio, cenca patla
oac inj atlapal: inj suchio to
maoac, iztac, viac, amo velic 
amo hiia, amo ine conj: in a
qujn quj necuj, ia ca chacha
qua chivi, ia ca tomaoa. Injc 
acan monequj: qujl quj moto

naltica, in tecpan cioa, in ca cal
tzacutoca; inj cio aoan catca mote
cu coma: qujl ic tlalticpac tlamat
que; ic tetzo tzonaloque, in qujn pi
aia in suchitla, yoan in cioa.(928)

Toch nacaz oacal suchitl, çan  
qualton, velic, aviac, hineconj, 
qualli, iectli.(929)

Tlapalho a cal suchitl; chichil
tic, çan  qualton, tlacotli, tetonal
tilonj; njc no tonaltia, njc no techtia, 
njc nomaca.
Chilqualli.(930)

Vitzpal suchitl.(931)

Ocoma cuj tlapil suchitl

in toztla tzompili.(933)

mjo.(934)

Omj suchitl: tlacotl, pipitzaoac 

         fo. 195

quj io io suchio: inj suchio iztac
qua mala cachton, tzim pitzaoac

Tlapal omj suchitl: ca no iehoatl

motlappoiava.(936)

Tlil suchitl, mecatic, me mecatic,

tetzitzilin, mo vico manj, moiaca
tlacanj, exoio, inj exoio xoxoctic:

Meca suchitl: xivitl, atlan atenco

Co atzon te coma suchitl: iuh

Aca suchitl tolpa tlactic, xexel

Quauh aca suchitl.(940)

Quauh izte suchitl, qua viz

Xala cocotli: tlacotl, iticoion

Ocelo suchitl: xivitl, inj atlapal

Quaz tal suchitl: tlaco tontli: inj

Vitzitziltetl: inj toca itech quj ca 
in vitzitzili, io an tetl: ipampa in 
itlachieliz, iuh qujn ma vitzitzilin 
iiviio, in mj toa totoz catleton. In 
itla chieliz iuh qujn ma centzon

iuh qujn tlatla, itech cen quj ca,

chiltic, in xoxoctic, in xiuh tototl, 
in tlauh quechol, in ca mopalli, in 
tlavitl, in qujltic. etc. çan  tetl atle 
itech ca tliltic: injn mj mjl tontli, 
iuh qujn icel azcatl tacapitz tontli,
can qualton, çan  tepiton; ompa 
ichan, ompa neci in teuatenco, il
hujca axaltitlan, in motta, io an 
ompa in toto nacapan atoiac,

valtica in neci. iuh qujn icpiton 
xotlatica; anoce iuh qujn çan  de
laton tlatlatica, in tla çan  valne
neci ca icpitl: auh in tlacan ie ca, 
in tlacan ie tlatlatica, ca iehoatl 
in vitzitziltetl, chipavac, atic, nal

tlamavicoltic, xoxoltla, pepetla

ca qual neci, chipaoaca neci, at
ca neci.(1035)
